It has come to our attention that there has been a significant increase in staff leave rates compared to last month. This is a serious concern, as it affects the smooth functioning of our operations and may lead to parent complaints.

Considering these factors, moving forward, your leave patterns will be closely monitored. Please be aware that your annual increment and other benefits may be impacted by your punctuality and attendance at work.

It is mandatory for all staff to submit supporting documents for any type of leave. Failure to provide the required documentation will result in the leave being treated as Loss of Pay (LOP). Please note that the total number of LOP days accumulated throughout the year will be considered during your performance evaluation.

We kindly urge all staff to refrain from taking unnecessary leave.

Thank you for your understanding and cooperation.

✨𝐋𝐞𝐚𝐝 𝐰𝐢𝐭𝐡 𝐢𝐧𝐭𝐞𝐧𝐭𝐢𝐨𝐧
The title on your email signature will fade, designations will shift, that corner office, large cabin, and latest tech are great, but the impact you leave on people will last forever ✨

⏳ 𝐓𝐢𝐦𝐞 𝐚𝐧𝐝 𝐡𝐞𝐚𝐥𝐭𝐡 𝐚𝐫𝐞 𝐲𝐨𝐮𝐫 𝐦𝐨𝐬𝐭 𝐯𝐚𝐥𝐮𝐚𝐛𝐥𝐞 𝐚𝐬𝐬𝐞𝐭𝐬
These are finite and precious, so prioritize them, as they are hard to recover once lost.

🤝𝐍𝐮𝐫𝐭𝐮𝐫𝐞 𝐫𝐞𝐥𝐚𝐭𝐢𝐨𝐧𝐬𝐡𝐢𝐩𝐬 𝐭𝐡𝐚𝐭 𝐚𝐥𝐢𝐠𝐧 𝐰𝐢𝐭𝐡 𝐲𝐨𝐮𝐫 𝐯𝐚𝐥𝐮𝐞𝐬
Family isn’t always blood. It’s crucial to connect with those who uplift you and minimize/avoid those who deplete your energy. 

🧘‍♀️𝐅𝐨𝐜𝐮𝐬 𝐨𝐧 𝐩𝐞𝐫𝐬𝐨𝐧𝐚𝐥 𝐠𝐫𝐨𝐰𝐭𝐡
When you look within and become self aware, you will find you need less external validation to feel worthy. 

💰𝐅𝐢𝐧𝐚𝐧𝐜𝐢𝐚𝐥 𝐢𝐧𝐝𝐞𝐩𝐞𝐧𝐝𝐞𝐧𝐜𝐞 
Follow the thumb rule of using 50% of your income for ‘needs’, 30% for wants, and 20% to savings and investments. And remember to set up minimum six months of your pay cheque as emergency fund. 

🎯𝐒𝐭𝐚𝐲 𝐭𝐫𝐮𝐞 𝐭𝐨 𝐲𝐨𝐮𝐫 𝐬𝐭𝐚𝐧𝐝𝐚𝐫𝐝𝐬
The more you say ‘no’ to distractions and external noise, the closer you’ll get to what truly matters.

🌟 This New Year, I choose to follow the inner compass that will uncover just one step at a time and that would be enough to trust and follow🌟

Wishing you a blessed, peaceful, and abundant New Year 2025 💫

•	Max Time :1 Minute

•	Individual players (one from each school).

25/02/2025, 19:34 - Hr Woodlem Poornima: Since you have the SIM card, you have control over the number, and you can regain access to Telegram. Here are your options to change the Telegram account linked to your number:

Option 1: Log in to Your Telegram Account on the Same Number
	1.	Uninstall Telegram from your device and reinstall it to clear any existing session.
	2.	Open Telegram and select “Start Messaging.”
	3.	Enter your phone number (the one linked to the new SIM card).
	4.	Request a login code – Telegram will send an SMS or a call to your number.
	5.	Enter the code to access your account.
	6.	If another person is using this number for Telegram, they will be logged out once you log in.

Option 2: Delete the Other Person’s Account (If You Want a Fresh Start)
	1.	Go to Telegram Deactivation Page
	2.	Enter your phone number and confirm with the code Telegram sends.
	3.	Follow the instructions to delete the existing account.
	4.	Once deleted, reinstall Telegram and register a new account with the same number.

Option 3: Contact Telegram Support (If You Face Issues)

If you cannot log in or receive the code, you can contact Telegram Support:
	1.	Visit Telegram Support
	2.	Submit a request explaining that you own the number and want to reclaim your account.

Since you have the SIM, you are the rightful owner of the number, and once you log in, the previous user will be logged out automatically.
